            var powerautomateProductHostnames = ["www.powerautomate.cn", "gov.flow.microsoft.us",
                "high.flow.microsoft.us",
                "high.flow.microsoft.us",
                "portal.flow.eaglex.ic.gov",
                "portal.flow.microsoft.scloud",
                "www.powerautomate.cn"];
            var hostName = window.location.host;
            return (powerautomateProductHostnames.includes(hostName) || hostName.indexOf("flow.microsoft.com") != -1);

class="lp-iframe-window" name="lp_iframe_chatwindow" id="lp_iframe_chatwindow" allow="camera;microphone" src="https://publisher.liveperson.net/iframe-le-tag/iframe-cs.html?lpsite=60270350&amp;lpsection=powerautomate-presales-en-us&amp;buttons=lpPowerPlatform"> </iframe> <div class="modal-wrapper-mask"><section id="lp-proactive-chat" class="section modal text-center lp-north-america" tabindex="0" aria-live="polite" aria-label="Chat now modal"> <div class="row lp-proactive-chat-body"> <div class="column"> <h3 class="text-heading3">Need Help?</h3> <p>Chat with a Microsoft sales specialist for answers to your Power Automate questions.</p> </div> </div> <div class="row lp-proactive-chat-buttons"> <div class="column"> <a id="lp-chatnow-button" href="#" target="_blank" class="button button-default  button-default--whiteonblack" role="button" aria-label="Chat now to get help with Power Automate"> <span>Chat now</span> </a> <a id="lp-chatnow-cancel-button" href="en-us/#" target="_blank" class="button button-default  button-default--blackonwhite" aria-label="No thanks, I don't need to chat."> <span>No thanks</span> </a> </div> </div> </section></div> <iframe sandbox="allow-scripts allow-same-origin" title="Adobe ID Syncing iFrame" id="destination_publishing_iframe_mscom_0" name="destination_publishing_iframe_mscom_0_name" src="https://mscom.demdex.net/dest5.html?d_nsid=0#https%3A%2F%2Fpowerautomate.microsoft.com" style="display: none; width: 0px; height: 0px;" class="aamIframeLoaded"></iframe><script>
         $(function () {
            var iframe = document.getElementById('lp_iframe_chatwindow');
            var proactiveChat = '#lp-proactive-chat';
            var closeButton = '#lp-modal-close';
            var chatButton = '.chat-button';
            var proactiveChatNowButton = '#lp-chatnow-button';
            var proactiveChatNowCancelButton = '#lp-chatnow-cancel-button';
            var chatButtonContainerSelector = '.chat-button-container';
            var currentFocus = ':focus';
            var lpIsInitialized = false;
            var lpConsentRequired = false;

            var enableChatButton = function () {
                $(chatButtonContainerSelector).removeClass('hidden').attr('aria-hidden', false);
                if (lpConsentRequired === false && lpIsInitialized === false) {
                    sendMessage({ action: 'initializeLP' })
                    lpIsInitialized = true;
                }
                sendMessage({ lppagename: document.title });
                sendMessage({ lpcurl: location.href });
            }

            // Method for sending messages to the iframe
            var sendMessage = function sendMessage(msg) {
                iframe.contentWindow.postMessage(msg, 'https://publisher.liveperson.net');
            }

            window.addEventListener('message', function (event) {
                if (event.origin === 'https://publisher.liveperson.net' && event && event.data) {
                    var src = event.data.action || event.data.window || event.data.engagement || event.data.button || event.data.invite;
                    switch (src) {

                        case 'ready':
                            sendMessage({ action: 'parentsize', Height: window.innerHeight, PixelRatio: 1, Width: window.innerWidth }); // This tells the iframe the available dimensions for the chat window.  This is especially important for mobile deployments.
                            break;

                        case 'maximized': // When maximized is passed from the iFrame we expect it to contain window dimensions, if it's mobile we'll be setting vh values, otherwise we're setting px values.  Both need to be assigned to the iFrame container.
                            iframe.style.width = event.data.width;
                            iframe.style.height = event.data.height;

                            if (event.data.height === '100vh') { // Mobile styling, detected by vh being passed vs px
                                iframe.style.position = 'absolute';
                                iframe.style.right = '0';
                            } else { // Desktop styling
                                iframe.style.position = 'fixed';
                                iframe.style.bottom = '0';
                                iframe.style.right = '0';
                                iframe.style.boxShadow = '0 0 6px rgb(214, 214, 214)';
                            }
                            break;

                        case 'minimized': // When minimized is passed the iframe should be hidden, it is important that your team add a button to restore the minimized chat like store currently does after this command is passed.
                            iframe.style.width = event.data.width;
                            iframe.style.height = event.data.height;

                            iframe.style.position = 'fixed';
                            iframe.style.bottom = '0';
                            iframe.style.right = '0';
                            iframe.style.boxShadow = '0 0 6px rgb(214, 214, 214)';
                            break;

                        case 'closed': // This command is passed when the chat is closed, you do not need to add a restore button and you should recieve a
                            iframe.style.width = event.data.width;
                            iframe.style.height = event.data.height;
                            break;

                        case 'opened': // This command is lets you know the window is opened, this usually occurs as the user navigates between pages while a chat is occuring.
                            iframe.style.width = event.data.width;
                            iframe.style.height = event.data.height;
                            break;

                        case 'buttonReady': // this lets us know that a button is on the page and ready to be clicked.
                            enableChatButton();
                            break;

                        case 'buttonNotReady':
                            $(chatButtonContainerSelector).addClass('hidden').attr('aria-hidden', true);
                            break;

                        case 'displayed': // This command should trigger your pages invite (ie Proactive Chat)
                            triggerChatModal();
                            break;

                        default:
                            break;
                    }
                }
            });

            window.addEventListener('resize', function (el) {
                // We utilize this to provide updates to the iFrame so the window can be resized if needed.  An example of this would be the user reducing the height of the browser below the height of the chat window.
                sendMessage({ action: 'parentsize', Height: el.target.innerHeight, PixelRatio: 1, Width: window.innerWidth });
            });

            $(chatButton).click(function (event) {
                event.preventDefault();
                sendMessage({ action: 'open' });
                sendMessage({ action: 'Topic', Topic: 'PowerAutomate' });
                sendMessage({ action: 'parentsize', Height: window.innerHeight, PixelRatio: 1, Width: window.innerWidth });
            });

            $(proactiveChatNowButton).click(function (event) {
                event.preventDefault();

                $(proactiveChat).trigger('hide.modal', ['lp-proactive-chat']);

                if (!lpIsInitialized) {
                    sendMessage({ action: 'initializeLP' });
                }

                sendMessage({ invite: 'accepted' });
                sendMessage({ action: 'Topic', Topic: 'PowerAutomate' });
                sendMessage({ action: 'parentsize', Height: window.innerHeight, PixelRatio: 1, Width: window.innerWidth });
            });

            $(proactiveChatNowCancelButton).click(function (event) {
                event.preventDefault();

                sendMessage({ invite: 'declined' });
                $(proactiveChat).trigger('hide.modal', ['lp-proactive-chat']);
            });

            /* Focus Trap */
            var tabCode = 9;
            var firstFocusableElement = $(closeButton);
            var lastFocusableElement = $(proactiveChatNowCancelButton);
            $(proactiveChat).keydown(function (event) {
                if (event.key == 'Tab' || event.keyCode === tabCode) {
                    if (event.shiftKey) {
                        if ($(currentFocus).is(firstFocusableElement)) {
                            lastFocusableElement.focus();
                            event.preventDefault();
                        }
                    } else {
                        if ($(currentFocus).is(lastFocusableElement)) {
                            firstFocusableElement.focus();
                            event.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }
                }
            });

            function triggerChatModal() {
                $(proactiveChat).trigger('show.modal', ['lp-proactive-chat']);
                $(closeButton).focus();
            };
        });
    </script> <div class="modal-wrapper-mask"><section id="modal-contact-us" class="section section-size0 modal modal-large modal modal-contact-us focus-trap partner_model" data-backdrop="static"> <div class="mc-contact-us-close-container"> <button id="modal-form-close-button" class="close x-hidden-focus" aria-label="close the form"> × </button> </div> <div class="mc-contact-us-container__content__heading hide-for-large"> <div> <span class="icon icon-size2"><img src="/images/application-logos/svg/powerautomate.svg" data-fallback="/images/application-logos/png/powerautomate.png" class="" role="presentation" alt=" Power Apps powerautomate"></span> <span class="logo-header-text"> Power Automate </span> </div> </div> <div class="mc-contact-us-modal-container"> <div class="mc-contact-us-content-container"> <div class="mc-contact-us-content-container__heading show-for-large"> <span class="icon icon-size4"><img src="/images/application-logos/svg/powerautomate.svg" data-fallback="/images/application-logos/png/powerautomate.png" class="" role="presentation" alt=" Power Apps powerautomate"></span> </div> <div class="mc-contact-us-content-container__description"> <h2 class="text-heading1" data-min-width="medium"> How can we help? </h2> <p class="text-body3"> Contact a Microsoft partner to: </p> <div class="mc-contact-us-content-container__description__items"> <ul> <li> <p> See a live demo. </p> </li> <li> <p> Set up a free trial. </p> </li> <li> <p> Get expert guidance on transforming business&nbsp;processes. </p> </li> <li> <p> Learn about purchase options, implementation and deployment. </p> </li> </ul> </div> </div> </div> <div class="mc-contact-us-form-container"> <div class="mc-contact-us-form-container__content"> <div class="mc-contact-us-form-content"> <form action="/en-us/forms/marketo-contact-us-form-submit/" class="text-left mc-contact-us-modal" data-form-type="contact-us" id="marketo-contact-us" method="post" novalidate="novalidate"> <fieldset> <script>

        var culture = "en-us";

        function onConsentChanged(e){
            if (!window.siteConsent.isConsentRequired) return;

            // Add a telemetry to know how many actually consent and what they consent to.
            if (appInsights && appInsights.trackEvent) {
                var consents = siteConsent.getConsent();
                appInsights.trackEvent({
                    name: 'onConsentChanged',
                    properties: { // accepts any type
                        Required: consents.Required,
                        Advertising: consents.Advertising,
                        SocialMedia: consents.SocialMedia,
                        Analytics: consents.Analytics
                    }
                });
            }

            window.location.reload();

            if (global && global.CookieHelper && global.CookieHelper.cleanNonEssentialCookies) {
                global.CookieHelper.cleanNonEssentialCookies();
            }

            $('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 'slow');
        }

        $(document).ready(function(){
            $("#footer-manage-cookie").click(function (ev) {
                ev.preventDefault();
                if (window && window.siteConsent && window.siteConsent.manageConsent) {
                    window.siteConsent.manageConsent();
                }
            });

            WcpConsent.init(culture, "cookie-banner", function (err, _siteConsent) {
                if (err != undefined) {
                    if (appInsights && appInsights.trackException) {
                        appInsights.trackException({
                            exception: err,
                        });

                    return;
                }

                    window.siteConsent = _siteConsent;

                    // if consentRequired is true, we will show the manage cookies
                    if (window.siteConsent.isConsentRequired) {
                        if ($("#wcf-consent-li") && $("#wcf-consent-li").length) {
                                $("#wcf-consent-li").show();

                            global.CookieHelper.cleanNonEssentialCookies();
                        }
                    }
                }
            }, onConsentChanged);
